    if tonumber(game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild(r0_482).Level.Value) < tonumber(r1_482) then

function getServerTime()
  -- line: [67, 69420] id: 659
  RealTime = tostring(math.floor(game.Lighting.ClockTime * 100) / 100)
  RealTime = tostring(game.Lighting.ClockTime)
  RealTimeTable = RealTime:split(".")
  Second = tonumber((0 + tonumber(RealTimeTable[2] / 100))) * 60
  Minute = RealTimeTable[1]
  return Minute, Second
end

function TweenTempleLegit()
  -- line: [67, 69420] id: 389
  AllNPCS = getnilinstances()
  for r3_389, r4_389 in pairs(game:GetService("Workspace").NPCs:GetChildren()) do
    table.insert(AllNPCS, r4_389)
  end
  for r3_389, r4_389 in pairs(AllNPCS) do
    if r4_389.Name == "Mysterious Force" then
      TempleMysteriousNPC1 = r4_389
    end
    if r4_389.Name == "Mysterious Force3" then
      TempleMysteriousNPC2 = r4_389
    end
  end
  r7_0(TempleMysteriousNPC2.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame)
  wait(0.5)
  if (TempleMysteriousNPC2.HumanoidRootPart.Position - game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Position).Magnitude < 15 then
    game.ReplicatedStorage.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("RaceV4Progress", "TeleportBack")
  end
  if (TempleMysteriousNPC1.HumanoidRootPart.Position - game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Position).Magnitude < 15 then
    game.ReplicatedStorage.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("RaceV4Progress", "Teleport")
  end
end

  end
end

function CheckMoon()
  -- line: [67, 69420] id: 504
  moon8 = "http://www.roblox.com/asset/?id=9709150401"
  moon7 = "http://www.roblox.com/asset/?id=9709150086"
  moon6 = "http://www.roblox.com/asset/?id=9709149680"
  moon5 = "http://www.roblox.com/asset/?id=9709149431"
  moon4 = "http://www.roblox.com/asset/?id=9709149052"
  moon3 = "http://www.roblox.com/asset/?id=9709143733"
  moon2 = "http://www.roblox.com/asset/?id=9709139597"
  moon1 = "http://www.roblox.com/asset/?id=9709135895"
  moonreal = MoonTextureId()
  cofullmoonkothangbeo = "Bad Moon"
  if moonreal == moon5 or moonreal == moon4 then
    if moonreal == moon5 then
      cofullmoonkothangbeo = "Full Moon"
    elseif moonreal == moon4 then
      cofullmoonkothangbeo = "Next Night"
    end
  end
  return cofullmoonkothangbeo
end

            wait(0.1)
            game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("StartQuest", NameQuest, LevelQuest)
          end
        elseif game:GetService("Players").LocalPlayer.PlayerGui.Main.Quest.Visible == true then
          checklevel()
          if game:GetService("Workspace").Enemies:FindFirstChild(Mon) then
            pcall(function()
              -- line: [67, 69420] id: 633
              for r3_633, r4_633 in pairs(game:GetService("Workspace").Enemies:GetChildren()) do
                if r4_633.Name == Mon then

                      HealthMin = r4_633.Humanoid.MaxHealth * _G.Kill_At / 100
                      local r5_633 = r4_633.Humanoid.Health
                      local r6_633 = HealthMin
                      if r5_633 <= r6_633 then
                        EquipWeaponGun()
                        ATween(r4_633.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, 10, 0))
                        r4_633.Humanoid.WalkSpeed = 0

                        r4_633.Head.CanCollide = false
                        r5_633 = {}
                        r5_633[1] = r4_633.HumanoidRootPart.Position
                        r5_633[2] = r4_633.HumanoidRootPart

                      else
                        AutoHaki()
                        EquipWeapon(_G.SelectWeapon)
                        r4_633.Humanoid.WalkSpeed = 0
                        r4_633.HumanoidRootPart.CanCollide = false
                        r4_633.Head.CanCollide = false
                        r4_633.HumanoidRootPart.Size = Vector3.new(50, 50, 50)
                        ATween(r4_633.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, 34, 4))
                        game:GetService("VirtualUser"):CaptureController()
                        r5_633 = game:GetService("VirtualUser")
                        r5_633:Button1Down(Vector2.new(1280, 672))
                      end
                      StartMasteryGunMagnet = true
                      r5_633 = r4_633.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame
                      PosMonMasteryGun = r5_633

                      StartMasteryGunMagnet = false
                      game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("AbandonQuest")

function DropFruit()
  -- line: [67, 69420] id: 630
  game.Players.LocalPlayer.PlayerGui.Main.FruitInventory.Position = UDim2.new(10.1, 0, 0.1, 0)
  game.Players.LocalPlayer.PlayerGui.Main.FruitInventory.Visible = true
  local r0_630 = game.Players.LocalPlayer.PlayerGui.Main.FruitInventory.Container.Stored.ScrollingFrame.Frame
  wait(0.3)
  for r4_630, r5_630 in pairs(r0_630:GetChildren()) do
    if string.find(r5_630.Name, "-") then
      for r9_630, r10_630 in pairs(game:GetService("Players").LocalPlayer.Backpack:GetChildren()) do
        FruitStoreF = string.split(r10_630.Name, " ")[1]
        FruitStoreR = FruitStoreF .. "-" .. FruitStoreF
        if r5_630.Name == FruitStoreR then
          game:GetService("Players").LocalPlayer.Backpack:FindFirstChild(r10_630.Name):Destroy()
        end
      end
    end
  end
  for r4_630, r5_630 in pairs(r0_630:GetChildren()) do
    if string.find(r5_630.Name, "-") then
      for r9_630, r10_630 in pairs(game:GetService("Players").LocalPlayer.Character:GetChildren()) do
        FruitStoreF = string.split(r10_630.Name, " ")[1]
        FruitStoreR = FruitStoreF .. "-" .. FruitStoreF
        if r5_630.Name == FruitStoreR then
          game:GetService("Players").LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild(r10_630.Name):Destroy()
        end
      end
    end
  end
end
